4658<h1 class="jupiterx-main-header-post-title" itemprop="headline">

4659How to Read (and Understand) a Cannabis Batch Label</h1>

4660<ol class="breadcrumb" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BreadcrumbList">

4661<li class="breadcrumb-item" itemprop="itemListElement" itemtype="http://schema.org/ListItem" itemscope="itemscope">

4668<li class="breadcrumb-item" itemprop="itemListElement" itemtype="http://schema.org/ListItem" itemscope="itemscope">

4669<a href="https://papaandbarkley.com/learn/category/cannabis-farmers/" itemprop="item">

4670<span itemprop="name">

4671Cannabis Farmers</span>

4672</a>

4673<meta itemprop="position" content="2" />

4674</li>

4675<li class="breadcrumb-item" itemprop="itemListElement" itemtype="http://schema.org/ListItem" itemscope="itemscope">

4682<li class="breadcrumb-item active" aria-current="page" itemprop="itemListElement" itemtype="http://schema.org/ListItem" itemscope="itemscope">

4683<span itemprop="name">

4684How to Read (and Understand) a Cannabis Batch Label</span>

4685<meta itemprop="position" content="4" />

4690<div class="jupiterx-main-content">

4691<div class="container">

4692<div class="row">

4693<div id="jupiterx-primary" class="jupiterx-primary col-lg-9">

4694<div class="jupiterx-content" role="main" itemprop="mainEntityOfPage" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/Blog">

4695<article id="32908" class="jupiterx-post post-32908 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-cannabis-farmers category-cannabis-industry tag-cannabinoids tag-cannabis-batch-label tag-cannabis-coa tag-coa tag-ecs tag-full-spectrum tag-heavy-metals tag-testing tag-whole-plant" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting" itemprop="blogPost">

4696<header class="jupiterx-post-header">

4697</header>

4698<div class="jupiterx-post-body" itemprop="articleBody">

4699<div class="jupiterx-post-content clearfix" itemprop="text">

4700<p>

4701<img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-32911" src="https://papaandbarkley.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/ibrkifvsqywakgssatab_acp8c9.jpg" alt="" width="1498" height="998">

4702</p>

4703

4704<p class="has-normal-font-size">

4705By: Laine Hammer &amp; Cyrus Sepahbodi Have you ever looked at your Papa &amp; Barkley product box and wondered, “How much THC is in this?” or “What is this label with the tiny numbers and letters?” We’ve had that same reaction, and<strong>

4706&nbsp;we’re here to provide some clarity on batch labels and teach you how to read them</strong>

4707. To get the best information possible about our particular Papa &amp; Barkley batch labels, we chatted with the Director of Logistics, Michael Heinstein and he explained why we use batch labels, what customers should look for when reading them, and why it’s all necessary for safe and transparent cannabis wellness products. Let’s get right down to it. All of the information on Papa &amp; Barkley’s batch labels is vital for us, and more importantly for you (the consumer!). Why? Because we want to be sure you know exactly what you’re getting in each and every product.</p>

4708

4709<div class="wp-block-spacer" style="height: 20px" aria-hidden="true">

4710 </div>

4711

4712<h2 class="has-primary-color has-text-color" id="h-what-you-should-look-for-on-a-cannabis-batch-label">

4713What You Should Look For On a Cannabis Batch Label</h2>

4714

4715<p class="has-normal-font-size">

4716Accurately reading a cannabis batch label is crucial to understand how each product will interact with your body. Pay attention to the cannabinoids, whether it has been tested, and if you have more questions, you can always contact the manufacturer to learn more. When you do reach out, the ID’s are critical to note so that you can reference it for specifics about your product. “It is important to note the total THC and total CBD within the product, to make sure they’re accurate and your dosage is correct. We want people to know that we always aim for a certain goal. It is also important to make sure you are looking at the batch label so you know exactly what you are applying to your skin or ingesting.” –&nbsp;<strong>

4717<em>

4718Michael Heinstein, Director of Logistics, Papa &amp; Barkley</em>

4719</strong>

4720</p>

4721

4722<div class="wp-block-spacer" style="height: 20px" aria-hidden="true">

4723 </div>

4724

4725<h2 class="has-primary-color has-text-color" id="h-breaking-down-a-papa-barkley-batch-label">

4726Breaking Down a Papa &amp; Barkley Batch Label</h2>

4727

4728<div class="wp-block-spacer" style="height: 20px" aria-hidden="true">

4729 </div>

4730

4731<div class="wp-block-image">

4732<figure class="aligncenter size-large">

4733<img loading="lazy" width="333" height="498" src="https://papaandbarkley.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cannabis_batch_label1_zhfs1e_qttezk.png" alt="" class="wp-image-32912" />

4734</figure>

4735</div>

4736

4737<div class="wp-block-spacer" style="height: 20px" aria-hidden="true">

4738 </div>

4739

4740<p class="has-normal-font-size">

4741<strong>

4742A Batch Label is a sticker on the side of the packaging that tells you:</strong>

4743</p>

4744

4745<ul>

4746<li>

4747Total mg count of cannabinoids in the package</li>

4748<li>

4749Cannabinoid count per serving</li>

4750<li>

4751Serving size</li>

4752<li>

4753Batch #</li>

4754<li>

4755Best By Date</li>

4756<li>

4757Manufacturing Date</li>

4758<li>

4759Packaged Date</li>

4760<li>

4761Tested Date</li>

4762<li>

4763Manufacturing license</li>

4764<li>

4765Which third-party lab tested the product</li>

4766</ul>

4767

4768<p class="has-normal-font-size">

4769Batch labels are relative to every product that is made by Papa &amp; Barkley. The info on the Batch Label comes from that product batch’s&nbsp;<a href="https://papaandbarkley.com/learn/how-to-read-a-cannabis-testing-coa/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">

4770Certificate of Analysis</a>

4771&nbsp;(COA). The cannabis testing COA is a document that outlines the testing results of a cannabis product. It details the contents of each product –&nbsp;from cannabinoid potency, terpenes content, residual solvents, pesticides, and heavy metals. Third-party testing helps us ensure that every product is as clean as can be and allows us to accurately create our batch labels.</p>

4772

4773<div class="wp-block-spacer" style="height: 25px" aria-hidden="true">

4774 </div>

4775

4776<h5 id="h-what-our-batch-label-means-from-top-to-bottom">

4777WHAT OUR BATCH LABEL MEANS FROM TOP TO BOTTOM:</h5>

4778

4779<div class="wp-block-spacer" style="height: 25px" aria-hidden="true">

4780 </div>

4781

4782<p class="has-normal-font-size">

4783<strong>

4784Total mg count of cannabinoids in the package&nbsp;</strong>

4785is important so you know how potent your product is and if the advertised cannabinoid count matches the testing COA. In the image above this 30:1 Tincture has 407.29 mg of CBD and 13.55 mg of THC. <strong>

4786Cannabinoid count per serving&nbsp;</strong>

4787is crucial to knowing how much total THC and total CBD is in each serving of the product, so your dosage is accurate for your needs and tolerance level. On our label you can see that each serving contains 6.78 mg CBD and 0.22 mg of THC per serving. <strong>

4788Serving size&nbsp;</strong>

4789is knowing how much you should take for the desired amount of THC and CBD. The standard serving per container is 0.25ml and there are 60 servings in the entire bottle. <strong>

4790Batch #:&nbsp;</strong>

4791Regulations require that all cannabis products are tested in batches. The batch ID refers to the specific product in your hand and identifies it from seed to sale. Of particular note, you’ll notice the letters ‘TN’ in the batch id: 082819<strong>

4792TN</strong>

4793002. This is referencing that it is a tincture. <strong>

4794Best By Date:&nbsp;</strong>

4795This section of the batch label serves as a measure for how long the product is at full strength. Regulations state that cannabis products must show a best by date of within one year. Because Papa &amp; Barkley utilizes a whole plant process for our products, they last significantly longer than what the regulation outlines. <strong>

4796Manufacturing Date:&nbsp;</strong>

4797This refers to when the batch was actually manufactured, meaning when the balm, tincture, or body oil was placed into its vessel. <strong>

4798Packaged Date:&nbsp;</strong>

4799When the product is placed in its final packaging. <strong>

4800Tested Date:&nbsp;</strong>

4801This refers to the exact date when the batch was tested by a certified third-party cannabis testing lab, such as our partners&nbsp;<a rel="noreferrer noopener" href="https://www.sclabs.com/" target="_blank">

4802SC Labs</a>

4803&nbsp;and&nbsp;<a rel="noreferrer noopener" href="https://csalabs.com/" target="_blank">

4804CannaSafe</a>

4805. Third-party testing labs are crucial to ensuring clean cannabis. We go above and beyond regulations to ensure each product meets our clean standards by triple-testing each batch throughout the process. <strong>

4806Manufacturing/Distribution Licenses:&nbsp;</strong>

4807These refer to the manufacturing and distribution licenses of the company that made the product (aka us!) The specific manufacturing license refers to the actual&nbsp;<strong>

4808building&nbsp;</strong>

4809where the product was made and its physical location. <strong>

4810Logo of which third-party lab tested the product:&nbsp;</strong>

4811Identifies the certified third-party cannabis testing lab that did the testing as a quality assurance measure. <a rel="noreferrer noopener" href="https://cannabis.ca.gov/2018/12/10/30056/" target="_blank">

4812California State regulation</a>

4813&nbsp;requires that the total THC and the total CBD are listed on each label. But, depending on the type of product, the levels of THC will vary. For a product such as our&nbsp;<a href="https://papaandbarkley.com/product/releaf-tinctures/">

481430:1 CBD-Rich Tincture</a>

4815&nbsp;(pictured above).</p>

4816

4817<div class="wp-block-spacer" style="height: 20px" aria-hidden="true">

4818 </div>

4819

4820<h2 class="has-primary-color has-text-color" id="h-clean-cannabis-means-transparency">

4821Clean Cannabis Means Transparency</h2>

4822

4823<p class="has-normal-font-size">

4824So, why are all these numbers and letters necessary to put on our packaging? Well, it starts with transparency. A batch label tells us everything we need to know about the product for complete traceability from soil to shelf. We believe it’s important that you know exactly what you’re putting in your body and that you’re getting the best product possible. Next time, pay attention to the label with the tiny numbers and letters because now you know how to read a batch label and make more informed decisions about the cannabis you consume. Avoid any products that do not have a batch label or companies that are unable or unwilling to provide a verified COA. We believe that education is vital, and Papa &amp; Barkley is happy to be your partner in cannabis wellness. If you love to do your research and want to dive deeper, you can easily request a COA for any of our products by emailing&nbsp;<a href="/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#a3cbc6cfd3e3d3c2d3c2c2cdc7c1c2d1c8cfc6da8dc0ccce">

4825<span class="__cf_email__" data-cfemail="dcb4b9b0ac9cacbdacbdbdb2b8bebdaeb7b0b9a5f2bfb3b1">

4826[email&#160;protected]</span>

4827</a>

4828.</p>

4829
